   <script>
    // banner下拉菜单显隐藏
		$(".banner-item:first, .banner-item:last").on("mouseenter", function () {
			jQuery(this)
				.children(".hideNav")
				.show();
			jQuery(this)
				.find(".arrowToBottom")
				.hide();
			jQuery(this)
				.find(".arrowToTop")
				.show();
		});
		$(".banner-item:first, .banner-item:last").on("mouseleave", function () {
			jQuery(this)
				.children(".hideNav")
				.hide().find(".hideNav-item a").removeClass("hover");
			jQuery(this)
				.find(".arrowToBottom")
				.show();
			jQuery(this)
				.find(".arrowToTop")
				.hide();
		});

		// 下拉菜单标签高亮
		$(
			".hideNavwrap:eq(0) a,.hideNavwrap:eq(1) a,.hideNavwrap:eq(2) a,.hideNavwrap:eq(3) a"
		).on("mouseover", function () {
			jQuery(this)
				.addClass("hover")
				.parent()
				.siblings()
				.children("a")
				.removeClass("hover");
		});
   </script>

  <script>
   //获取地址栏参数，name:参数名称
	function getUrlParam(name) {
		var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)");
		var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
		if (r != null)
			return unescape(r[2]);
	}

	var addressUrl = window.document.URL;
	var pageType = 1;//首页
	if (window.document.URL.indexOf(window.document.domain + '/CATList-')) {
		pageType = 2;//列表页
	} else if (window.document.URL.indexOf('/ART-')) {
		pageType = 3;//详情页
	}

	var url = "//ad.ofweek.com/advertising/getAd/1/0/1";
	var data = {};
	var preZoneId = getUrlParam("preZoneId");
	if (preZoneId != undefined && preZoneId != "") {
		data = {
			"preZoneId" : preZoneId
		};
	}
	jQuery.ajax({
		url : url,
		data : data,
		dataType : "JSONP",
		jsonp : "callback",
		jsonpCallback : 'successCallback'
	});
	function successCallback(resp) {
		var fr = true;
		if (resp.code == "1") {
			var data = resp.data;
			var infomationFlowAd = [];
			var reg = new RegExp("^[0-9]*$");
			for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
				//区域标识id为数字，表示信息流广告
				if (reg.test(data[i].zoneIdentification)) {
					//console.log("信息流");
					infomationFlowAd.unshift(data[i]);
				} else if (data[i].zoneIdentification == ""
						|| data[i].zoneIdentification == undefined) {
					if (jQuery != undefined) {
						jQuery("body").append(data[i].content);
					} else {
						$("body").append(data[i].content);
					}
				} else if (data[i].zoneIdentification == "template_bottom_expo_ad") {
					var html = '<li ';
					if (fr) {
						html += 'class="fr"';
					}
					fr = false;
					html += '><a href="'+ data[i].adLink +'" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">\
						<img src="'+ data[i].imagePath +'" />\
					</a>\
				</li>';

					if (data[i].monitorLink != ""
							&& data[i].monitorLink != undefined) {
						html += '<script src="' + data[i].monitorLink + '"><\/script>';
					}
					if (jQuery != undefined) {
						jQuery("#template_bottom_expo_ad").append(html);
						if (jQuery('.news-layout-twenty-one'))
							jQuery('.news-layout-twenty-one').show();

					} else {
						$("#template_bottom_expo_ad").append(html);
						if ($('.news-layout-twenty-one'))
							$('.news-layout-twenty-one').show();
					}
				} else if (data[i].zoneIdentification == "template_top_suspension_ad") {
					if (jQuery != undefined) {
						jQuery("body").prepend(data[i].content);
					} else {
						$("body").prepend(data[i].content);
					}
				} else {
					if (jQuery != undefined) {
						jQuery("#" + data[i].zoneIdentification).append(
								data[i].content);
					} else {
						$("#" + data[i].zoneIdentification).append(
								data[i].content);
					}
				}
			}
			if (infomationFlowAd.length > 0) {
				window.infomationFlowAd = infomationFlowAd;
				pushMesAd();
			}
		} else {
			console.log("get Ad EOR");
		}
		
	}

	//添加信息流广告
	function pushMesAd() {
		var id = '0';
		var divObj = null;
		//ai
		if (id == "201700") {
			divObj = $('.main-cont-left .content');
			//氢能 、储能、智慧城市、云计算、新材料
		} else if (id == "180800" || id == "180200" || id == "201800"
				|| id == "178800" || id == "180400") {
			divObj = $('.article-con .article-item');
		}
		if (divObj) {
			while (infomationFlowAd.length > 0) {
				var ad = infomationFlowAd.pop();
				var index = ad.zoneIdentification;
				var adhtml = getInfomationFlowAd(ad);
				divObj.eq(index - 1).after(adhtml);
			}
		}
	}

	function getInfomationFlowAd(ad) {
		var adhtml = bigclassAdhtml(ad);
		return adhtml;
	}

	function bigclassAdhtml(ad) {

		var advertiser = ad.advertiser;
		if (!advertiser) {
			advertiser = "";
		}
		var id = '0';
		var resultHtml = "";
		if (id == "201700") {//人工智能
			resultHtml = '<div class="content">'
					+ '<div class="item-box  clearfix">'
					+ '<div class="item-box-left">'
					+ '<a class="wid-img"  title="'+ad.title+'"  href="'+ad.adLink+'"><img src="'+ad.imagePath+'" alt="'+ad.title+'"/></a>'
					+ '</div>'
					+ '<div class="item-box-right clearfix">'
					+ '<div class="top-title mtl15">'
					+ '<a href="'+ad.adLink+'"  title="'+ad.title+'"  target="_blank">'
					+ ad.title
					+ '</a>'
					+ '</div>'
					+ '<div class="box-right-text clearfix">'
					+ '<div class="box-right-text-left">'
					+ '<a href="'+ad.adLink+'" target="_blank">'
					+ '<span class="blue" style="vertical-align: middle;">'
					+ advertiser
					+ '</span>'
					+ '<div class="ad-tag" style=" display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left:10px;"><img src="//www.ofweek.com/images/group2.png" alt="广告"></div>'
					+ '</a>' + '</div>' + '<div class="box-right-text-right">' +
					//'<div class="share">'+
					//'<p class="social-share" data-sites="weibo,qq,qzone,wechat" data-url="'+ad.adLink+'" data-title="'+ad.title+'"></p>'+
					//'</div>'+
					'</div>' + '</div>' + '</div>' + '</div>' + '</div>';
		} else if (id == "180800" || id == "180200" || id == "201800"
				|| id == "180400") {//氢能 、储能、智慧城市、新材料
			resultHtml = '<div class="article-item">'
					+ '<a href="'+ad.adLink+'" target="_blank"><img src="'+ad.imagePath+'" alt="'+ad.title+'"></a>'
					+ '<div class="detail" style="height:128px;position:relative;">'
					+ '<h2><a href="'+ad.adLink+'" target="_blank">' + ad.title
					+ '</a></h2>' + '<p class="time"><span></span></p>' +

					'<h5 style="position:absolute;bottom:0;left:0;">'
					+ '<a href="'+ad.adLink+'" target="_blank">'
					+ '<span class="tag-advertiser">' + advertiser + '</span>'
					+ '<span class="label"><img src="//www.ofweek.com/images/group.png" alt="广告" style="vertical-align: middle;width:35px;height:18px;"></span>' + '</a>' + '</h5>'
					+ '</div>' + '<div class="sharebar">' +
					//'<i class="iconfont icon-share" ></i>'+
					'</div>' + '</div>';
		} else if (id == "178800") {//云计算
			resultHtml = '<div class="article-item">'
					+ '<a href="'+ad.adLink+'" target="_blank"><img src="'+ad.imagePath+'" alt="'+ad.title+'"></a>'
					+ '<div class="detail">'
					+ '<h2><a href="'+ad.adLink+'" target="_blank">' + ad.title
					+ '</a></h2>' + '<p class="time"><span></span></p>' +

					'<h5>'
					+ '<a href="'+ad.adLink+'" target="_blank">'
					+ '<span class="label" style="color:#16CFF7;">' + advertiser + '</span>'
					+ '<span class="label"><img src="//www.ofweek.com/images/group.png" alt="广告" style="vertical-align: middle;"></span>' + '</a>' + '</h5>'
					+ '</div>' + '<div class="sharebar">' +
					//'<i class="iconfont icon-share" ></i>'+
					'</div>' + '</div>';
		}
		return resultHtml;
	}
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   welcomeAd = {
            show: function () {
                var $ad = jQuery('#welcomeAd');
                var w = $ad.width();
                var h = $ad.height();
                var hw = ('-'+h/2+'px 0 0 '+'-'+w/2+'px');
                $ad.css({
                    display: 'block !important',
                    left: '50%',
                    top: '50%',
                    margin: hw
                })
                jQuery('body').addClass('hidden-all');
            },
            hide: function () {
                var $ad = jQuery('#welcomeAd');
                $ad.hide();
                jQuery('body').removeClass('hidden-all');
            }
        }

        setTimeout(function () {
            welcomeAd.hide();
        }, 8000);

        // 欢迎广告需要在body上添加：class="hidden-all"
        welcomeAd.show();
        
     // 对联广告滚动显示
        var left1_flag = true;
        var rb_flag = true;
        jQuery(window).scroll(function () {
            var top = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
            if (top > 600) {
                if (left1_flag) {
                    jQuery('#ad-duilian-left').show();
                    jQuery('#duiliandl-right1').show();
                }
                if (rb_flag) {
                    jQuery('#ad-right-bottom-fuchuang').show();
                }
            } else {
                jQuery('#ad-duilian-left').hide();
                jQuery('#duiliandl-right1').hide();
                jQuery('#ad-right-bottom-fuchuang').hide();
            }
        });
        jQuery('body').on('click', '#ad-duilian-left .closed', function () {
            left1_flag = false;
        });
        jQuery('body').on('click', '#ad-right-bottom-fuchuang .ad-close-btn', function () {
            rb_flag = false;
        });
  </script>

		$node.eq(i).attr("src",$node.eq(i).attr("data-src"));
	}
}
